 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh has said that the National Counter Terrorism Center (NCTC) is very important to tackle terrorism
 rajyon ke mukhyamantriyon ke saath baithak main pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne kaha ki ensitisi centre or rajyon ke bich kaa koi jhagada nahin he or na hi yah rajyon ke adhikaron main dakhal he
 He said that the NCTC will increase the ability to fight terror
 rajdhani ke vigyaan bhawan main yojit baithak main manmohan singh ne kaha ki desh ke liye kanoon bananaa centre sarkaar kaa kaam he
 He said that there is need for cooperation from the State Government on this issue
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne rajya sarkaron se kaha ki ve aatankwaad se nipatane main kendra ke saath rahen
 The country will have to establish a strong national vision and strategy to deal with terrorism
 ensitisi par mukhyamantriyon ke sammelan kaa udghaatan karte hue manmohan singh ne kaha, ‘aatankwaad aaj hamaari rashtriya suraksha ke liye sabase bade khataron main se he
 There is no disagreement that an effective anti-terrorism system should be created and that the effective system and counter system should be at both the national and state levels
 ’unhone kaha ki ensitisi kii avadharana mantri samooh or prashasnic sudhaar ayog kii ore se aayi, jinhone kargil main mili sabak ke baad kaam shuru kiya
 Manmohan Singh said, "we believe that the NCTC will strengthen the counter-terrorism capabilities of the states, including their nature and operational aspects, rather than digging their roots
" manmohan singh ne mukhyamantriyon kaa dhyaan maanak karrwai prakriya (esaopi) kii ore aakarshith kiya, jiskaa masauda kendriya grih mantralay ne vitarit kiya he
 The Prime Minister said that the draft reflects the organizational structure of the NCTC and the detailed provisions for coordination between the Center and the state regarding its proposed rights and functioning
 pradhanmantri ne kaha, ‘ensitisi sucharu or prabhaavshaalee rup se kaam kar sake, iske liye mahatvapurn baat yah he ki iske adhikaron or kaamkaaj ko lekar hamaare bich aam sahmati bane
 We would like the state governments to join us in this initiative
 hamaara maananaa he ki aatankwaad rodhi prayaason ko ensitisi or majboot karegaa
 In this meeting called after about 12 chief ministers opposed to the formation of NCTC, Manmohan Singh said that the mechanism of NCTC will give every state agency the ability to see the larger scenario of terrorist threat and it will strengthen the anti-terrorism capabilities
 pradhanmantri ne sangheey dhaanche ko nuksaan pahunchane kii kuch mukhyamantriyon kii ashankaon kaa niraakaran karte hue kaha ki sarkaar kaa iraadaa kisi bhi tarah se samvidhan main pradutt kendra or rajyon ke bich adhikaron ke vitaran ko prabhavit nahin karnaa he
 He said that both the Center and the state cannot fight terrorism on their own
 unke bich najdiki sahyog or samanvay aavashyak he taaki seemaa ke bheetar or baahar se hone vaale khataron se nipta ja sake
 Manmohan Singh said that it is the responsibility of the Center to shape a strong national vision and strategy, based on the information received from all over the world and from our states
 unhone kaha ki rajyon ko apni ore se yahi karnaa he ki ve apni visheshgyata, gyaan or tantra kaa upyog apane kshetron kii suraksha ke liye karen or kendra tathaa anya rajyon ke saath milakar kaam karen
 Manmohan Singh said that since the terrorist attack in Mumbai in November 2008, there has been close coordination between the states and the central agencies so far, which has led to huge successes, though much more remains to be done
 unhone kaha ki kul milakar bharat main seemaa paar ke aatankwaad, vampanthi ugravad, jammu kashmir ke aatankwaad, purvottar ke ugravad or dharm aadhaarit aatankwaad sahit bharat main aatankwaad ke sabhi ayaamon se nipatane ke liye ranneeti or upayon ko lekar hamaare bich vyapak sahmati he

 chidambaram ne kaha ki aatankwaad se ladanaa centre or rajyon kii saajha jimmedaari he

 unhone kaha ki NCTC ke sabhi pahaluon par vichaar hua he
 Chidambaram said that there was a change in UAPA in 2008, but no question was raised then

 Read the profile of Justice Rajinder Sachcher Justice Rajinder Satcher was born on 22 December 1923
 unke pita kaa naam bhim sen sachhar tha
 He did his studies from Lahore
 diavi hiskool, government college lahore or lau college lahore se unhone padhai kii

 12 farvari 1970 ko rajinder sachhar 2 saal ke liye dilli hai court ke adishnal jaj niyukt kiye gaye

 bharat ne rwanda ke saath apane rishton ko majboot kiya he, ise purvi africa ke pravesh-dwaar ke rup main dekha ja rahaa he or isi ke maddenjar pichley saal janvari main bharat ne rwanda ke saath ranneetik saajhedaari kii
 While briefing the media about the Prime Minister's visit, Secretary (economic Relations) in the Ministry of External Affairs, T
 es
 Tirumurthy said, "india will soon begin its first mission in Rwanda, India's current High Commissioner for Rwanda is in Kampala, Uganda
 " bharat ne rwanda ko 40 karod dollar kaa karj diya he or vahaan bharat kii ore se prashikshan chaatravruti kaarykram chalaae ja rahe hai
 Two agreements are expected to be signed during Modi's visit in which $ 100 million will be provided for an industrial park and the same amount will be provided for agriculture and irrigation projects
 thirumurti ne kaha, "ham raksha, deyari sahyog, chamada, krishi or samskruti ke kshetra main bhi anubandh hone kii ummid karte hai
 "in Rwanda, Modi will visit the Ravuru Model Village and provide a gift of 200 cows as a part of the program under the supervision of President Kagame
 vahaan sarkaar kii ore se nirdhantam pariwaron ko deyari ke liye gaayen di jaati he or bhaichara badhaane ke liye gaay kii pehali bachhiya log apane padosi ko uphaar ke rup main dete hai
 Modi will arrive in Uganda on July 24 from Rwanda, the first bilateral visit by the Indian Prime Minister in the last 21 years
 thirumurti ne bataaya ki bharat or uganda ke bich raksha sahyog badhaane ke liye prashikshan or kshamta nirmaan par dhyaan diya jayega, vahaan zinja main 2010 se bhartiya sena kaa prashikshan dal tainaat he
 After meeting with Ugandan President Yoovei Museveni and delegation-level talks, Modi will attend the joint trade program between India and Uganda
 bharat ke pradhanmantri pehali baar uganda kii sansad ko sambodhit karenge
 The Prime Minister will also address members of the Indian community in Uganda
 thirumurti ne kaha, "hamen ummid he ki uganda ko bijli line or sab-stesan ke liye 14
 1 million dollars and 6 for agriculture and dairy production
 4 karod dollar pradaan kiye jaaenge
 "modi will arrive in South Africa from Uganda on 25 July at the end of his tour
 bricks shikhar sammelan ke alaava, modi farvari main dakshin africa kii satta sanbhaalane vaale raashtrapati siril ramafosa ke saath dwipaksheeya vaarta karenge
 The 10th summit of BRICS leaders is taking place in South Africa, with the theme 'cooperation of developing countries for inclusive growth and shared prosperity in the Fourth Industrial Revolution'
 bricks sammelan main africa deshon ke aamantrit samooh main rwanda, uganda, togo, jambia, namibia, senegal, gaban, ithopia, angola or african union chair shaamil hai, anya aamantrit deshon main argetina, turki, indonesia, jamaica or misr shaamil hai
 On the sidelines of the BRICS summit, Modi will also meet Chinese President Xi Jinping there
 yah donon netaaon ke bich ek saal ke bheetar teesri mulaakaat hogi

 or dekhie imran ko bhi kashmir yaad aa hi gaya

 har pakistani par kareeb dedh lakh rupee kaa karz he or mulk ke paas udhaar chukaane ke liye paise tak nahin
 But this is the helplessness of Pakistan
 bina kashmir kaa naam liya unka khaanaa hazam nahin hota he
 Imran Khan Sepakistan is not being run
 lekin kashmir par bolne main wo usee tarah se aage hai

 kashmir ke naam par ek baar phir vahi purana tepe bajane laga he

 naa to pakistan nayaa hua or naa hi dhimi arthvyavastha main raftaar ai
 Imran Khan's country has been forced to walk on the opposite knee
 paise paise ko mohataaj pakistan se mulk ke 20 karoda log to sanbhal nahin rahe hai
 Despite this, wazir-e-azam Imran Khan needs a solution to the Kashmir issue from the UN
 pakistan ke pradhanmantri imran khan kah rahe hai 'ham 'IOK' (bharat kaa kashmir) main maasoom kashmiriyon kii hatya kii kadi ninda karte hai
 The time has come when India should understand that a solution to the Kashmir issue can only come out of negotiations which should include the proposal of UN SC and the will of Kashmiris
 'pradhanmantri banane se pehle or pradhanmantri banane ke fouran baad imran khan nae pakistan ke nae rishton kii baat karte rahe the
 So it felt like something would change in Pakistan
 lekin dhak ke vahi teen paat hai
 The country stands on the basis of hatred
 usase ummid bhi auki kya kii ja sakati he
 Ever since Pakistan has been singing the ragas of Kashmir
 tab se hindustan pakistan ko samajha rahaa he ki agar kashmir par baat kerani he to aamane saamne hogi
 India will not tolerate any third on this issue
 lekin baatcheet bhi tab hi hogi
 When Pakistan will shut down its terror factories and stop the supply of terrorists
 haalanki kaayade se hamaari ummid hi galat thi
 Because Imran Khan has always stood with the Taliban
 unka upnaam hi taliban khan tha
 But now Pakistan is also issuing postage stamps in memory of the terrorists killed in Kashmir
 matlab saaf he paise se bhalepakistan kangalho
 Corruption along with poor economy, unemployment is at its peak
 magar use apni janata ko gumraah karne ke liye kashmir mudda hi suhaata he
 So the new captain has also adopted the same tactic
 army kii badaulat imran khan kursi par to baith gaye
 But Pakistan has not managed them
 or ye ham nahin khud pakistani netaa kah rahe hai
 Imran Khan spread the trap of talking about peace in the name of new Pakistan
 wo dhire dhire sabake saamne aa chukaa he
 Today, he is putting petrol in his own fire
 piem banate hi wo aman chaiyn kii baaten kar rahe the
 But this should be the trap of Imran Khan
 yaa phir unke aakaa general bajva kii aatanki chaal
 India knows the vein of Pakistan
 jisamen dhokhe ke alaava kuch or nahin he
 But now the age of this deception is over
 cinemagharon main raashtragan ke maamle par sunwaayee karte hue supreme court ne apane aadesh par roak lagane or use waapas lene se inkaar kar diya he
 The court also clarified things on its old order
 supreme court ne saaf kiya ki kisi cinema, newsril yaa dacumentary main raashtragan kaa istemaal kiya gaya he to logon ko khadey hone kii jarurat nahin he
 The Supreme Court also made it clear that people will have to stand in theaters during the national anthem, but it is not necessary that they sing the national anthem
 bataa den ki centre sarkaar ne supreme court ke aadesh kaa samarthan kiya
 During the hearing in court in the case, Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi said, "this question is to show the patriotic spirit of the citizens of the country
" jab ise lekar koi kanoon nahin he to supreme court kaa aadesh ahm ho jaataa he
 The national anthem should be mandated in all schools except theaters as the spirit of patriotism should be introduced to children
 vahiin, supreme court main is aadesh ko lekar daakhil yachikaaon main kaha gaya he ki is aadesh ko waapas len kyonki ye aadesh adhikaron kaa hanan karte hai
 The court should not apply this to entertainment places like cinema
 is maamle kii agali sunwaayee 18 april ko hogi
 The Supreme Court held a major hearing on the national anthem
 pichley 30 november ko supreme court ne raashtragan, yani 'jan gana man' se jude ek ahm antarim aadesh main kaha tha ki deshbhar ke sabhi cinemagharon main film shuru hone se pehle raashtragan bajegaa
 The Supreme Court also said that it would be mandatory to show the national flag on the screen of the cinema hall while playing the national anthem, and all those present in the cinema hall would have to stand in honor of the national anthem
 supreme court ne kaha ki raashtragan rashtriya pahchaan, rashtriya ekta or sanvaidhanik deshbhakti se judaa he
 According to the court order, it should be kept in mind that the national anthem cannot be used in any commercial interest
 iske alaava kisi bhi tarah kii gatividhi main drama creat karne ke liye bhi raashtragan kaa istemaal nahin hoga, tathaa raashtragan ko vairieti song ke taur par bhi nahin gaaya jayega
 In fact, the petition by Shyam Narayan Chokse said that the practice of the national anthem should be banned for any commercial activity, and that the national anthem should not be used to create drama in entertainment shows
 yachika main yah bhi kaha gaya tha ki ek baar shuru hone par raashtragan ko ant tak gaaya janaa chahie, or bich main band nahin kiya janaa chahie
 The petition also urged the court to order that the national anthem should not be sung among people who do not understand it
 iske atirikt raashtragan kii dhun badalakar kisi ore tareeke se gane kii ijazat nahin milani chahie
 The petition said that in such cases the national anthem is in violation of the rules and it is against the 1971 law
 isse pehle, supreme court ne is yachika par sunwaayee karte hue centre sarkaar ko notice jari kar jawaab maanga tha
 The comments supreme court ne kaha tha ki jab log raashtragan or rashtriya dhvaj kaa aadar karenge to isse logon ke man main deshbhakti or rashtrawaad kii bhaavana jagegi
 The Supreme Court said that it is the fundamental duty of these people to respect and follow the constitution and then to honor constitutional institutions, the national anthem and the national flag
 supreme court ke justise deepak mishra kii bench ne ye bhi kaha tha ki ye baat saaf he ki sabhi nagarikon kaa daayitv he ki vah samvidhan ke adarsh ko maane
 The court had said that it is the need of the hour that the citizens of the country feel that they live in the country and their duty is to honor the national anthem which is a symbol of constitutional patriotism and nationality
 vyaktigat soch ke naam par is maamle main aazaadee nahin di ja sakati
 There is no place for personal thinking here
 sanvaidhanik adarsh ke tahat ye sweekaarya nahin he
 At the same time, the petitions filed in the Supreme Court regarding this order have been asked to withdraw this order as these orders violate the rights
 court ko cinema jaise intertenment jagahon par ye lagu nahin karnaa chahie
 The matter will be next heard on 18 April
 supreme court main raashtragan ko lekar aham sunwaayee hui
 Last November 30, the Supreme Court had said in an important interim order related to the national anthem, 'jana Gana Mana', that the national anthem would be played before the film started in all theaters across the country
 supreme court ne yah bhi kaha ki raashtragan bajte samay cinemahol ke parde par rashtriya dhvaj dikhaaya janaa bhi anivaary hoga, tathaa cinemaghar main maujuud sabhi logon ko raashtragan ke sammaan main khadaa hona hoga
 The Supreme Court held that the national anthem is associated with national identity, national unity and constitutional patriotism
 court ke aadesh ke mutabik, dhyaan rakhaa jaae ki kisi bhi vyavsaayik hit main raashtragan kaa istemaal nahin kiya ja saktaa
 Apart from this, the national anthem will not be used to create drama in any kind of activity, and the national anthem will not be sung as Variety Song either
 darasal, shyaam narayan chaukase kii yachika main kaha gaya tha ki kisi bhi vyavsaayik gatividhi ke liye raashtragan ke chalan par roak lagaai jaani chahie, or antertenment sho main drama creat karne ke liye raashtragan ko istemaal na kiya jaae
 The petition also stated that once started the national anthem should be sung to the end, and not stopped in between
 yachika main court se yah aadesh dene kaa aagrah bhi kiya gaya tha ki raashtragan ko aise logon ke bich na gaaya jaae, jo ise nahin samajhate
 Apart from this, changing the tune of the national anthem should not allow singing in any other way
 yachika main kaha gaya ki is tarah ke maamalon main raashtragan niyamon kaa ulanghan he or yah varsh 1971 ke kanoon ke khilaaf he
 Earlier, the Supreme Court, hearing this petition, issued a notice to the Central Government seeking an answer
 tippaniyan The Supreme Court had said that when people respect the national anthem and the national flag, it will inculcate the spirit of patriotism and nationalism in the minds of the people
 supreme court ne kaha ki ye logon kii fundamental duty he ki vah samvidhan kaa aadar karen or uskaa paalan karen or phir sanvaidhanik sansthaanon, raashtragan or rashtriya dhvaj kaa sammaan karen
 The bench of Supreme Court Justice Deepak Mishra also said that it is clear that it is the duty of all citizens to follow the ideals of the Constitution
 adaalat ne kaha tha ki samay kii maang he ki desh ke naagarik mahasoos karen ki vah desh main rahete hai or unki duty he ki vah raashtragan kaa sammaan karen jo ki sanvaidhanik deshbhakti or rashtriyata kaa pratik he
 Freedom in this matter cannot be given in the name of personal thinking

 The relationship between the US and Pakistan is at its worst this time
 aarthik madad par roak ke baad america or pakistan ke bich kii duuri badhati ja rahi he
 After the US stopped the financial assistance to Pakistan, India's neighboring country had given a hint that it would not allow American supplies to Afghanistan to be routed through its route
 ab america ne bhi hint diya he ki vah pakistan ke raste se jane ke bajaae anya vaikalpik root par sambhaavnaaen talash rahaa he
 When asked, what would America do if Pakistan was not going to let the US military and other supplies go through its path to Afghanistan, angry with the financial help being stopped
 jaaniye wo chaar kaaran jisaki vajah se trump ne pakistan kii nakel caseeis sawaal ke jawaab main america adhikari steven goldstin ne kaha, "america madhya asian deshon se baat kar rahaa he yaa phir vah rus kii ore se saamaan kii supplai bhejne kii koshish karegaa
 There may be some alternative routes if Pakistan closes its doors
 "america ne haal hi main pakistan ko die jane vaale 2 arab dollar kii madad par roak laga di he, jiske baad donon deshon main tanatani kaa maahaul dekha ja rahaa he
 He said, "this suspension is not completely cut off
 nai madad nahin di jaaegi or hamen ummid he ki pakistan bhavishya main hamaare saath sahyog karegaa
 "the US says that Pakistan will continue to hold until it takes strict action against the Haqqani terrorist network and the Afghan Taliban

 Now once again this situation seems to be in front of America
 pakistan kii ore se apni simaaen roke jane kii sthiti main america agar nae root talashta he to yah uske liye kaaphi kharchila hoga

 3 overon kii saajhedaari kar team ko shuruaati jhatkon se ubaara or uske baad riddhimaan saaha ke saath chathe wicket ke liye 108 ranon kii naabad saajhedaari nibhaakar unhone bharat ko sankat se baahar nikaal liya
 His partnership with Rahane was 39 runs
